    <script src="/webcomponents-lite.min-2c53f523.js"></script>
    <script>
      window.Polymer = {lazyRegister: true};
    </script>
    <script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
      window.XH = window.XH || {};

      window.XH.locale = {
        determine: function() {
          var appLocale = localStorage.language;
          var browserLocale = window.navigator.userLanguage ||
            window.navigator.language;

          // Ignore browser locale if it's not a supported language
          var supportedLocales = ['en-US', 'es-US'];
          if (!appLocale && supportedLocales.indexOf(browserLocale) === -1) {
            browserLocale = undefined;
          }

          var locale = appLocale || browserLocale || 'en-US';

          if (locale === 'es-US') {
            document.getElementById('message').textContent = 'Conectando ahora con su casa';
          }

          return locale;
        }
      };

      (function() {
        function getParameterByName(name) {
          name = name.replace(/[\[\]]/g, "\\$&");
          var regex = new RegExp("[?&]" + name + "(=([^&#]*)|&|#|$)");
          var results = regex.exec(window.location.href);
          if (!results) { return null; }
          if (!results[2]) { return ''; }
          return decodeURIComponent(results[2].replace(/\+/g, " "));
        }

        /**
         * Import the xh-app component compiled for the chosen locale
         */
        function loadLocalApp() {
          var APP_NAME = 'xh-app-7af98c71';
          var locale = window.XH.locale.determine();

          var link = document.createElement('link');
          link.rel = 'import';

          //
          // Load either the local app or a built asset bundle
          //
          if (document.domain == "local.home.xfinity.com" &&
            !(getParameterByName('branch') || getParameterByName('fp'))
          ) {
            if (getParameterByName('v')) {
              link.href  = '/' + locale + '/' + APP_NAME + '.html';
            } else {
              link.href = '/assets/xh-app/xh-app.html';
            }
          } else {
            var branch = getParameterByName('branch');
            var fingerprint = getParameterByName('fp');

            if(branch) {
              branch = 'http://xh-' + branch + '.g1.app.cloud.comcast.net/';
            } else {
              branch = '/';
            }

            if(fingerprint) {
              fingerprint = '/xh-app-' + fingerprint;
            } else {
              fingerprint = '/' + APP_NAME;
            }

            link.href  = branch + locale + fingerprint + '.html';
          }

          document.head.appendChild(link);
        }
        loadLocalApp();

        // remove splash and set loaded state
        document.querySelector('xh-app')
          .addEventListener('xh-app--loaded', function() {
            document.body.setAttribute('loaded', '');

            setTimeout(function() {
              var splash = document.querySelector('#xh-splash');
              splash.parentNode.removeChild(splash);
            }, 400);
          });
      })();
    </script>
